The EEA consists of countries in the European Union, Switzerland, Iceland, Liechtenstein and Norway: they are considered to have equivalent laws when it comes to data protection and privacy.  This kind of data transfer may happen if our servers (i.e. where we store data) or our suppliers and service providers are based outside the EEA, or if you use our services and products while visiting countries outside this area.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">If Vodafone sends your information to a country that is not in the EEA, we will make sure that your information is properly protected. We will always ensure that there is a proper legal agreement that covers the data transfer. In addition, if the country is not considered to have laws that are equivalent to EU data protection standards then we will ask the third party to enter into a legal agreement that reflects those standards.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="MuiPaper-root MuiPaper-elevation MuiPaper-elevation0 MuiAccordion-root MuiAccordion-gutters accordionItem mui-1ms8mr9"><div aria-controls="panel4-content" aria-expanded="false" class="MuiButtonBase-root MuiAccordionSummary-root MuiAccordionSummary-gutters accordionSummary mui-pfhti5" id="panel4-header" role="button" tabindex="0"><div class="MuiAccordionSummary-content MuiAccordionSummary-contentGutters mui-1j7w0la"><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 heading mui-18qmoti">How long we keep your personal information for</p></div><div class="MuiAccordionSummary-expandIconWrapper mui-160v3m0"><span class="iconButton MuiBox-root mui-1f8cx2n" role="img"></span></div></div><div class="MuiCollapse-root MuiCollapse-vertical MuiCollapse-hidden mui-a0y2e3" style="min-height:0px"><div class="MuiCollapse-wrapper MuiCollapse-vertical mui-hboir5"><div class="MuiCollapse-wrapperInner MuiCollapse-vertical mui-8atqhb"><div aria-labelledby="panel4-header" class="MuiAccordion-region" id="panel4-content" role="region"><div class="MuiAccordionDetails-root accordionDetails mui-1tco0e8"><div class="MuiBox-root mui-1r9o8lo"><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-1fw06gs">We’ll store your information for as long as we have to by law. If there’s no legal requirement for us to retain the data, we’ll only store it for as long as we need to.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="MuiPaper-root MuiPaper-elevation MuiPaper-elevation0 MuiAccordion-root MuiAccordion-gutters accordionItem mui-1ms8mr9"><div aria-controls="panel5-content" aria-expanded="false" class="MuiButtonBase-root MuiAccordionSummary-root MuiAccordionSummary-gutters accordionSummary mui-pfhti5" id="panel5-header" role="button" tabindex="0"><div class="MuiAccordionSummary-content MuiAccordionSummary-contentGutters mui-1j7w0la"><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 heading mui-18qmoti">Keeping your personal information secure</p></div><div class="MuiAccordionSummary-expandIconWrapper mui-160v3m0"><span class="iconButton MuiBox-root mui-1f8cx2n" role="img"></span></div></div><div class="MuiCollapse-root MuiCollapse-vertical MuiCollapse-hidden mui-a0y2e3" style="min-height:0px"><div class="MuiCollapse-wrapper MuiCollapse-vertical mui-hboir5"><div class="MuiCollapse-wrapperInner MuiCollapse-vertical mui-8atqhb"><div aria-labelledby="panel5-header" class="MuiAccordion-region" id="panel5-content" role="region"><div class="MuiAccordionDetails-root accordionDetails mui-1tco0e8"><div class="MuiBox-root mui-1r9o8lo"><div class="vdf-group col-xs-12 col-sm-10 col-lg-8 MuiBox-root mui-k9riyl"><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">We have specialised security teams who constantly review and improve our measures to protect your personal information from unauthorised access, accidental loss, disclosure or destruction.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">Communications over the internet (such as emails) aren’t secure unless they’ve been encrypted. Your communications may go through a number of countries before being delivered, as this is the nature of the internet.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">We cannot accept responsibility for any unauthorised access or loss of personal information that is beyond our control.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">We’ll never ask for your secure personal or account information by an unsolicited means of communication. You’re responsible for keeping your personal and account information secure and not sharing it with others.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">Our website may provide links to third-party websites. We cannot be responsible for the security and content of such third-party websites. So make sure you read that company’s privacy and cookies policies before using or putting your personal information on their site.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">The same applies to any third-party websites or content you connect to using our products and services.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">You may choose to disclose your information in certain ways such as social plug-ins (including those offered by Google, Facebook, Twitter and Pinterest) or using third-party services that allow you to post reviews or other information publicly, and a third party could use that information.</p><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">Social plug-ins and social applications are operated by the social network themselves and are subject to their own terms of use and privacy and cookies policies. You should make sure you’re familiar with these.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="MuiPaper-root MuiPaper-elevation MuiPaper-elevation0 MuiAccordion-root MuiAccordion-gutters accordionItem mui-1ms8mr9"><div aria-controls="panel6-content" aria-expanded="false" class="MuiButtonBase-root MuiAccordionSummary-root MuiAccordionSummary-gutters accordionSummary mui-pfhti5" id="panel6-header" role="button" tabindex="0"><div class="MuiAccordionSummary-content MuiAccordionSummary-contentGutters mui-1j7w0la"><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 heading mui-18qmoti">Your rights</p></div><div class="MuiAccordionSummary-expandIconWrapper mui-160v3m0"><span class="iconButton MuiBox-root mui-1f8cx2n" role="img"></span></div></div><div class="MuiCollapse-root MuiCollapse-vertical MuiCollapse-hidden mui-a0y2e3" style="min-height:0px"><div class="MuiCollapse-wrapper MuiCollapse-vertical mui-hboir5"><div class="MuiCollapse-wrapperInner MuiCollapse-vertical mui-8atqhb"><div aria-labelledby="panel6-header" class="MuiAccordion-region" id="panel6-content" role="region"><div class="MuiAccordionDetails-root accordionDetails mui-1tco0e8"><div class="MuiBox-root mui-1r9o8lo"><div class="vdf-group col-xs-12 col-sm-10 col-lg-8 MuiBox-root mui-k9riyl"><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">Under the law, you have a number of rights that you can exercise free of charge. We have included a summary of these below; if you would like to discuss or exercise any of these, please contact us through the details provided.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>Right to correct personal data</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">If you believe any of the personal data we hold about you is incorrect, you can request we update it.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>Right to access personal data</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">You have a right to request a copy of the information that we hold about you, and how it has been processed.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>Right to data portability</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">In some circumstances, you have the right to receive the personal information about you which you have provided to us, in a structured, commonly used and machine-readable format and have the right to transmit this data to a third party.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>Right to object to use of personal data</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">Where we are processing your data for the purposes of direct marketing, or any legitimate interests that Vodafone is reliant upon, you can object at any time to this processing.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>Right to restrict use of your data</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">In some circumstances, you can request that we temporarily suspend the processing of your data.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>Right to erasure</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">In some circumstances, such as where we no longer have a justifiable reason to continue to process your data, you can request we delete it.</p><h5 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h5 mixedFontWeight mui-oc9hat"><strong>How to lodge a complaint</strong></h5><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-gutterBottom mui-99auw5">If you have a complaint, you can contact us on the details provided. We’ll do our best to help but if you’re still unhappy, you can contact the ICO, which is the UK data protection regulator – their details are at <a href="http://www.ico.org.uk/">www.ico.org.uk</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div aria-labelledby="vdf-tab-1" class="tabPanel" hidden=""
